803 : RL 2.15 |RL 2.15: astitî silakrama.  sthiti
804 : RL 2.15 |RL 2.15: aṅanakĕn sañjata kosa-wahana niṅ ajurit. We have here a frequent use of kośa(wāhana), which as such seems to be unknown in Skt. Kośa is here: everything the troops need, stores, supplies. Kośawāhana (not to be taken as dwandwa) is then: everything which carries supplies for the troops (wagons, horses, etc), impedimenta, wagon-train. When preceded by bala it seems to be either: supplies, vehicles for the troops (HW 32.1;  AWj 42.3; Sut 96.7), or (bala + kośawāhana): troops and their supplies, fully equipped troops (GK 2.10). Semantically it comes close to kĕkĕs (q.v.), aṅĕkĕs, pakĕkĕs (equipment).  kośawāhana, (bala-kośawāhana
